📝 Common error meanings:
   • ImagePullBackOff - Pod trying to pull image from registry (should use local)
   • ErrImageNeverPull - pullPolicy: Never but image not in local (tag mismatch?)
   • CrashLoopBackOff - Pod started but crashed
   • Pending - Waiting for resources

Troubleshooting:
   1. Check which images are missing:
      docker image ls | grep job7189

   2. Check pod image configuration (what pods are trying to pull):
      kubectl get pod -n job7189-apps -o json | jq '.items[] | {name: .metadata.name, images: .spec.containers[].image}'

   3. Compare values file tags with actual build script tags:
      echo 'Values tags:' && grep -r 'tag:' k8s-management/values/
      echo 'Build script tags:' && grep 'IMAGE_TAGS' 04-build-and-push-images.sh -A 10

   4. Describe a failed pod for details:
      kubectl describe pod -n job7189-apps <pod-name>

   5. Check pod logs (if container started):
      kubectl logs -n job7189-apps <pod-name> --all-containers=true
